  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7e2d3b8a-06bb-472b-9736-65b0017cad94'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText5509207845456920662" style="display:none"><b>She’s addicted to sex. He’s addicted to booze…the only way out is rock bottom.</b><br /><br />No one would suspect shy Lily Calloway’s biggest secret. While everyone is dancing at college bars, Lily stays in the bathroom. To get laid. Her compulsion leads her to one-night stands, steamy hookups and events she shamefully regrets. The only person who knows her secret happens to have one of his own.<br /><br />Loren Hale’s best friend is his bottle of bourbon. Lily comes at a close second. For three years, they’ve pretended to be in a real relationship, hiding their addictions from their families. They’ve mastered the art of concealing flasks and random guys that filter in and out of their apartment.<br /><br />But as they sink beneath the weight of their addictions, they cling harder to their destructive relationship and wonder if a life together, for real, is better than a lie. Strangers and family begin to infiltrate their guarded lives, and with new challenges, they realize they may not just be addicted to alcohol and sex.<br /><br />Their real vice may be each other. <br /><br /><b>New Adult Romance recommended for readers 18+ for mature content</b></span>

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Yep :) It's possible to read Thrive (#2.5) in place of the Calloway Sisters spin-off series to shorten it down and therefore only read Lily & Lo's POV<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Yep :) It's possible to read Thrive (#2.5) in place of the Calloway Sisters spin-off series to shorten it down and therefore only read Lily &amp; Lo's POVs. We layout the multiple ways you can read the Addicted series on our Tumblr page: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://kbmritchie.tumblr.com/post/92557906772/could-we-read-the-new-spinoffs-coming-out-without">http://kbmritchie.tumblr.com/post/925...</a> <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11284813-christy?shelf=2019-audio">2019-audio</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer778427326" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12657417758652568233"><b>4.5 stars!</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504720999i/23807463.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Addicted to You</i> is a story that is just that- <b>addictive</b>. I can’t imagine finishing this book and not needing to dive right into the next. I can’t believe that I’ve waited this long to read this series, but I’m kind of glad I did. I can binge read them all now. :D <br/><br/>Lily and Lo are childhood friends and a couple as far as everyone knows. In reality, they’re both addicts. Lo is an alcoholic and Lily is a sex addict. They both come from rich, affluential families and if their families ever</span>
  <span id="freeText12657417758652568233" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars!</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504720999i/23807463.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Addicted to You</i> is a story that is just that- <b>addictive</b>. I can’t imagine finishing this book and not needing to dive right into the next. I can’t believe that I’ve waited this long to read this series, but I’m kind of glad I did. I can binge read them all now. :D <br><br>Lily and Lo are childhood friends and a couple as far as everyone knows. In reality, they’re both addicts. Lo is an alcoholic and Lily is a sex addict. They both come from rich, affluential families and if their families ever found out, it would be bad. So they pretend. They pretend to be a couple, pretend to be together to take the heat off one another. In reality, they are best friends and enablers for each others addictions. They are always there for each other and always have each other’s backs. Even if their relationship isn’t the healthiest, you can tell their friendship is real and so it the love between them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504720999i/23807464.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> “You’re a permanent fixture in my life. You're not going anywhere.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br>After carrying on this charade for years, something happens between this couple. They both come to realize their feelings are stronger than just friendship. They love each other as more than friends. Even with their addictions, they want to try. Try to turn what first started as a facade into something real. Become a real couple. Maybe Lo can drink less and maybe Lily can control her addiction to being only with Lo. Just maybe they can do this together… <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I want to love you more than I love this.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504720999i/23807465.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both of these characters are destructive, damaged and flawed. And I loved them both. Lo is such a fantastic guy- he had so many issues of his own but he loves Lily fiercely and wants her to be his. I adored him. I also loved all of the secondary characters- Ryke, Connor, even Rose by the end. I can’t wait to read more about them and I’m happy to know they’ll be getting their own books! <br><br>This story had such a unique plot. I loved that even though both of the main characters fed their addictions, they really did care about one another and honestly cared more about helping the others than helping themselves. By the end they learned sometimes you have to help yourself first before you can help the person you love. I have a feeling in <i>Ricochet</i> they will both face many challenges but I hope that their love will endure and pull them through battling their demons. The writing style was perfect- I couldn’t believe that this was written by two people, it had such a great flow. <i>Addicted to You</i> is the start of an intense, emotional, edgy and addictive series that you won’t want to miss out on! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1504720999i/23807466.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12657417758652568233" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_756010084" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/756010084" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/756010084?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18369048-addicted-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer756010084" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14701971199032478544"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383929531i/6706795._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383858801i/6688477.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383858801ra/6688479.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> WOW!!! I have found a new favorite series!!! <br/><br/>I swear it was like this book was written for me. It had all the elements I love in a story -- great writing, deeply flawed but lovable characters and an emotional intensity that kept drawing me further and further in. <br/><br/>I'm totally addicted ;) </b><br/><br/>The story is about Lily and Lo. They're childhood friends who have grown up together but they each have an addiction -- she's addicted to sex, he's addicted to booze -- and if their very wealthy and controlling </span>
  <span id="freeText14701971199032478544" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383929531i/6706795._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383858801i/6688477.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383858801ra/6688479.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> WOW!!! I have found a new favorite series!!! <br><br>I swear it was like this book was written for me. It had all the elements I love in a story -- great writing, deeply flawed but lovable characters and an emotional intensity that kept drawing me further and further in. <br><br>I'm totally addicted ;) </b><br><br>The story is about Lily and Lo. They're childhood friends who have grown up together but they each have an addiction -- she's addicted to sex, he's addicted to booze -- and if their very wealthy and controlling families ever found out, they'd both be kicked to the curb... and so they lie. They live together and pretend to be a normal, perfectly functioning couple and by doing so each one gives the other an alibi and a safe zone to feed their addiction.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"We lied for each other and hid our infidelities, playing the role of doting boyfriend and girlfriend. The deeper we sink, the harder it is to crawl out. I fear the moment when… someone discovers our secrets. At any moment, everything can crumble beneath us."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>But sometimes there are moments when their pretend relationship feels like the most real thing in the world because what neither of them are admitting out loud is that their feelings for each other <em>are</em> real.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"In this moment, I'm yours."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>By covering for each other and understanding what it was that they each needed, they'd found a way to cope with their addiction. It might not have been healthy but neither of them could stop and they found a balance, albeit a dangerous one, that worked for them... But everything changed when they were forced to go on a family yacht trip -- sequestered together away from any possibility of enabling their addictions in secret, the only thing they had was each other...<br><br>I'm going to stop here but seriously, I just LOVED the whole storyline. I felt so deeply invested in it and I read so many scenes with that butterflies-in-my-belly feeling. I don't know... there's just something about flawed, damaged characters who clearly love each other SO much and are trying as hard as they can do make it through something together that just strongly tugs at my heartstrings.<br><br>Both Lily and Lo were such intriguing characters. The whole story is told from Lily's POV and I really have to commend the authors with the way they were able to portray her addiction -- the vicious cycles, her need, her self loathing, her dependence on it. It would have been very easy to make Lily just seem like a slut but they wrote it in such a way that you could genuinely feel that this was an <em>addiction - </em>no different than drugs or alcohol. It wasn't just about someone who was promiscuous, this was something that was much more deeply wired in her.<br><br>And Lo... OMG Loren Hale totally stole my heart!! He was such a deeply tormented and flawed character and it was so clear how <em>much</em> he cared for Lil but I could also sense his inner conflict at not wanting to step in the way of what she needed while he himself was such a slave to his own addictions.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
<em>His voice lowers… "I don't have any right to tell you to stop...</em> <em>I'm here for you. Always."</em>
</blockquote>
</b><br>They were oddly perfect for each other. They each understood the deep seeded addiction the other suffered. They'd seen each other at their worst and the way they <em>cared</em> for each other (and I'm not even talking romantically, I just mean <em>caring</em> from one person to another) was just so incredible heart wrenching.... I mean, HOLY EMOTION!!!!<br><br>And all these hidden feelings were building in the background so by the time they actually took their relationship to the next level and officially became a couple, these feelings all came to the surface and I just <em>felt</em> it so strongly!!!!<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"I'm not one of your conquests," he says in a throaty voice. "I know what you want, and you don't need to take it. I can give it to you... Let me try," he says, his hand cupping my face. "Let me try to be enough for you."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>GAHHHH!!!!! That scene!!!!! I'm getting all emotional just thinking about it!! I love Loren Hale!! I love how much he loved Lily and how he didn't try and change her per say. It would have been so easy for a guy in his position to be jealous and irrational given the type of addiction she had but he accepted it all as a part of her. He didn't just love her and put up with her addiction, he accepted her as a package deal.<br><br>Ok - now, I know that some of you are going to be curious as to whether or not there is cheating in this (especially given Lily's addiction) and I'm happy to say that <em>no</em> - there is no cheating. However, before they're officially a couple she does sleep around but, with the way it was written, I totally understood it and Lo understood it too. This story just has totally different parameters than a normal romance would. But after they become a couple, there is no sleeping around at all.<br><br>Towards the ending, the emotions began to intensify as their addictions began to take a stronger hold of them. You could feel the breaking point coming and it hurt to see these characters who I loved so much falling so far. I cared <em>so</em> much for them but had to wait for them to save themselves. My heart goes right out to Lily and Lo and I can't wait to see them overcome the obstacles that I know will be their future. But I have faith in them and I believe that their love for each will be strong enough to get them through it.<br><br>While there isn't a brutal cliffhanger at the ending, it definitely leaves you wanting more <em>right away</em>!! Think kind of along the lines of a <i>Find You In The Dark</i> style ending.<br><br>But luckily the next books, <i>Ricochet</i> and <i>Addicted For Now</i> are both available so you'll have more of the story to immediately move on to.<br><br><strong>This series has me hooked!! I'm totally addicted and can't wait for more of Lily &amp; Lo! ♥</strong><br><br><strong>Rating: 4.5+ stars</strong><br><br><br><b>My review of Book #1.5 ➜ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1baSZSK">http://bit.ly/1baSZSK</a><br>My review of Book #2 ➜ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1baTdJG">http://bit.ly/1baTdJG</a><br>My review of Book #3 ➜ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/McHotQ">http://bit.ly/McHotQ</a><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14701971199032478544" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_874153428" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/874153428" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/874153428?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/24620157-addicted-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=childhood-loves">childhood-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=wtf-did-i-just-read">wtf-did-i-just-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer874153428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6234648198776391362">Well, this was certainly different! I've had this book sitting on my shelf for a long time. Finally, I got a chance to listen to it. I'm not quite sure what I expected, but this wasn't it. That isn't necessarily bad though. I'm still trying to wrap my head around this story.<br/><br/>First off, let me just say that both of the main characters are completely screwed up! Lily is a sex addict, sleeping her way through her early-twenties like there's no tomorrow. Meanwhile, Loren, aka "Lo", is drinking like a</span>
  <span id="freeText6234648198776391362" style="display:none">Well, this was certainly different! I've had this book sitting on my shelf for a long time. Finally, I got a chance to listen to it. I'm not quite sure what I expected, but this wasn't it. That isn't necessarily bad though. I'm still trying to wrap my head around this story.<br /><br />First off, let me just say that both of the main characters are completely screwed up! Lily is a sex addict, sleeping her way through her early-twenties like there's no tomorrow. Meanwhile, Loren, aka "Lo", is drinking like a fish. Both of them are completely out of control.<br /><br />Best friends since early-childhood, this dysfunctional duo is deserving of an after-school, Lifetime movie special. Holy hell, they were frustrating! Talk about co-dependent and enabling! These two needed some serious help.<br /><br />Oddly, it was their addictions that made them more human. Even though their behaviors were appalling, their weaknesses made them personable. Otherwise, I'm not sure that I ever would have been able to feel any sort of connection to the two trust fund babies. There was just nothing about their privileged lifestyle that I could relate to. Although addiction isn't something I can necessarily relate to either, it helped to see them as flawed humans that also have struggles.<br /><br />As their addictions spin more wildly out of control, circumstances change. Lily and Lo are willing to act on their feelings, even if it means risking what they have. One bad situation leads to another and the two cannot hide their problems any longer. <br /><br />While I enjoyed this story, I didn't love it. These two were a bit too dysfunctional for me at times. It does end without answering many questions, so I'll probably pick this series back up at some point. I hear that it gets better. After all, I am curious to see how these two manage on a more long-term basis. <br /><br />All in all, I'd say this was good, but not great. I give it 3 - 3 1/2 stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6234648198776391362" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_763047605" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/763047605" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/763047605?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3598635288" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1833794189050192556"><b>2.5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>me talking to myself before reading this book:</b><br/><br/>"im not gonna read this. nuh uh 😩👋🏼"<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603332185i/30270772.jpg' width='350' height='195' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>"no for real bishh don't read this. you read the blurb - h being a sex addict and H being an alcoholic. this will just stress you the f out. you have TWO midterms this week, sit your ass down and Don't You. Dare. read this or i-"<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603332225i/30270773.jpg' width='350' height='195' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"... i fucking read it."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603332225i/30270774.jpg' width='350' height='195' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>i SWORE to myself that i was just going to skim read this and only read the parts where Rose and Connor interact so im prepared for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20619577.Kiss_the_Sky__Calloway_Sisters__1_' title='Kiss the Sky (Calloway Sisters #1) by Krista Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kiss the Sky</a> but one</span>
  <span id="freeText1833794189050192556" style="display:none"><b>2.5 stars</b><br><br><b>me talking to myself before reading this book:</b><br><br>"im not gonna read this. nuh uh 😩👋🏼"<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603332185i/30270772.jpg" width="350" height="195" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>"no for real bishh don't read this. you read the blurb - h being a sex addict and H being an alcoholic. this will just stress you the f out. you have TWO midterms this week, sit your ass down and Don't You. Dare. read this or i-"<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603332225i/30270773.jpg" width="350" height="195" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"... i fucking read it."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603332225i/30270774.jpg" width="350" height="195" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>i SWORE to myself that i was just going to skim read this and only read the parts where Rose and Connor interact so im prepared for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20619577.Kiss_the_Sky__Calloway_Sisters__1_" title="Kiss the Sky (Calloway Sisters #1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss the Sky</a> but one thing lead to another and i ended up taking an 8 hour break from studying so alas here i am. <br><br>~ <b>went in for Rose and Connor, came out wanting to read the whole damn thing just to see more Rose, Connor and Ryke content</b> ~<br><br>aaand what do i have to say about Lily and Lo? well...<br><b>Lily</b> (a sex addict) + <b>Lo</b> (an alcoholic) = <b>T O X I C</b><br><br>i can't really rant about this book without spoiling so, <b>// SPOILERS AHEAD //</b><br><br>this whole book was a painful ✨mess✨ the first <b>39%</b> had a lot of OM drama and a little bit of OW drama for 2 chapters where Lily hears Lo with another girl, <b>Cassie</b> and that OW stayed with them for a week or something and then it was over. and as for OM drama well... she is a sex addict so she wasn't celibate. <br><br>AND THEN when they finally get together that's where all the toxic shit happens. <b>there were more bad than good</b> that happened here and most of the time i do feel bad but other times i get so frustrated because of how selfish they both are- especially Lily. but i can't exactly be <i>really</i> mad at them cuz of their addiction and well, selfishness is the reality for addiction so- everything is just COMPLICATED. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1603173176ra/30260725.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>again, it's really hard to like or even relate to the main characters and root for their relationship because <b>they both enabled each other's addictions</b> and <b>there's also not much depth to the characters</b> as they were all about their vices so that's why i couldn't connect with them. <br><br>also, i know Lily is suffering from her addiction but i feel so uncomfy whenever her mind wanders off and checks random guys out and creates sexual fantasies in her head and this happened a few times even when she and Lo were already together. i also feel uncomfy when <u>she finds it hard NOT to cheat</u> <br><br>despite all this, i can appreciate how the authors <i>showed</i> - not told - the struggles and negative aspects of what sex addicts go through and how it can impact friendships and family relationships. it felt real to me so that's why it was so painful to read. but again, there's A LOT more bad than good in this book in every sense so yeah it makes sense for every encounter to be painful. though, i just finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/55475465.Ricochet__Addicted__2_" title="Ricochet (Addicted #2) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Ricochet</a> now and lemme tell y'all- Lily's character development tho. YES.<br><br>➵ <b>
  <u>Connor and Rose + Ryke</u>
</b><br>alright, alright now let's talk about these three. FIRST of all.<br><br>— <b>Ryke:</b> i had no idea who he was before this but like... he can <i>get it</i>.<br>— <b>Connor:</b> <i>yes i do the cooking, yes i do the cleaning</i> 😌<br>— <b>Rose:</b> *bends the knee* MAH QUEEN.<br><br>i <i>really</i> can't wait to read Calloway series but these three really made me want to read the whole damn series. i literally have like- 3 books to get through before <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20619577.Kiss_the_Sky__Calloway_Sisters__1_" title="Kiss the Sky (Calloway Sisters #1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss the Sky</a>. rip.<br><br>aaand i was NOT expecting Ryke to be <i>that</i> to Lo. i loved him because he was supportive and seemed to care more about his well-being but... mind-fucking-BLOWN. it makes sense now why he's like that!!<br><br>if you ask me who i like more, Connor or Ryker? please don't ask me thx.<br><br>* * *<br><br>listen, listen. im a newbie to this whole fandom/series and i don't know <i>anyone</i> so bear with me. i originally wanted to just read the Calloway sisters series for Rose and Connor because i've been seeing tons of edits of them and i'm currently in a mood to binge read another series so i was like <i>ehh why not, it's not like i have exams and papers coming up and it's not like i have an exam in an hour or so right??</i> <br><br>anyway, stan Connor and Ryke for clear skin ✨<br><br><b>
  <u>Addicted series</u>
</b><br><b>#1: addicted to you</b> ↠ <i>2.5 stars</i><br><b>#2:</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3601751707" rel="nofollow noopener">ricochet</a> ↠ <i>3.25 stars</i><br><b>#3:</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3603804887" rel="nofollow noopener">addicted for now</a> ↠ <i>3.5 stars</i><br><b>#3:</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3603998691" rel="nofollow noopener">thrive</a> ↠ <i>tbr</i> <br><b>#5:</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3603998707" rel="nofollow noopener">addicted after all</a> ↠ <i>tbr</i></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1145537672" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1145537672?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover?shelf=i-m-not-crying-you-re-crying">i-m-not-crying-you-re-crying</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1145537672" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17518497324651281826"><b>
  <i>"He’s my drug that I gladly consume, and I think that’s what he fears most. He enables my addiction. Always has. And the longer we’re together, he always will.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436482503i/15466083._SY540_.jpg' width='450' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I LOVED THIS BOOK. I loved the characters, the writing, the storyline, how DIFFERENT it was from any other story I have read. It was emotional, heart breaking but refreshing, sometimes comical, full of drama, and also intense.<br/><br/>Lily and Lo- Lifetime friends. Addicts. Lovers. Liars. And two of the most dysfunctional/flawed but amazing c</span>
  <span id="freeText17518497324651281826" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"He’s my drug that I gladly consume, and I think that’s what he fears most. He enables my addiction. Always has. And the longer we’re together, he always will.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436482503i/15466083._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I LOVED THIS BOOK. I loved the characters, the writing, the storyline, how DIFFERENT it was from any other story I have read. It was emotional, heart breaking but refreshing, sometimes comical, full of drama, and also intense.<br><br>Lily and Lo- Lifetime friends. Addicts. Lovers. Liars. And two of the most dysfunctional/flawed but amazing characters I have met.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436482503i/15466084._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Lily is addicted to sex. Lo is addicted to alcohol. And they both use each other as a crutch to justify the addictions they cannot seem to control. They pretend to be a couple to their families, so they can continue to indulge in their addictions and not be questioned. After some time, they become a real couple, only to come to the conclusion that maybe they really aren’t that good for each other. Maybe feeding into one another’s addictions is only tearing them and their families apart.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436482503i/15466085._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I was a little hesitant when I started this, knowing something as serious and intense as addiction isn’t something that is considered easy to read about. But the writing and characters (ESPECIALLY the side characters) drew me in and kept me there.<br><br>I just love when I read a book and the characters begin to feel REAL to me. And that is precisely what happened here. It was like I could almost feel the love, the shame and guilt, the pain Lily &amp; Lo were feeling as they battled their addictions. And in the end it was beautiful and heartwarming to see how their family battled along side them. Even though their relationship was an unhealthy one, the love between Lily &amp; Lo will have you rooting for them to fight and get better.<br><br>I seriously cannot wait to dive into the rest of this series!<br><br>Addicted To You (Book 1) |<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/2zRYSYS">http://amzn.to/2zRYSYS</a><br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Find Me On:<br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thecrazyworldofabooklover/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/profile.php?id=100009277089211" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Page</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover/" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://twitter.com/_StephDeMarco_" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer6192147734004824122">|3.6 stars|<br/><br/>Since I'm on my phone, I'll just share my thoughts really quick.<br/> <br/>There's no doubt I will be reading the next books in the series but I don't know what to expect. It's safe to say I didn't like this book and I wasn't enjoying it until Connor showed up. <br/><br/>I understand what the author was trying to do and I admire how constant and somehow realistic her characters were. Like how Lily's addiction was delivered and her in between thoughts; I could feel her desperation and that was pretty cool</span>
  <span id="freeText6192147734004824122" style="display:none">|3.6 stars|<br /><br />Since I'm on my phone, I'll just share my thoughts really quick.<br /> <br />There's no doubt I will be reading the next books in the series but I don't know what to expect. It's safe to say I didn't like this book and I wasn't enjoying it until Connor showed up. <br /><br />I understand what the author was trying to do and I admire how constant and somehow realistic her characters were. Like how Lily's addiction was delivered and her in between thoughts; I could feel her desperation and that was pretty cool but I wish this book had been also from Loren's POV because, while I could sympathize a little with Lily, he was a total mistery until his breakdowns. I could not get a solid idea of Lo's character until more people were involved. <br /><br />As a couple Lily and Lo were absolutely auto-destructive and I was just waiting for it. Lily gave up, Lo gave up and I just didn't know how things were going to turn out. But like I said, Connor's arrival was, for me, the catalyst and Rose could get involved and so Ryke. <br /><br />I do like how the book ended. They weren't good for each other yet and they both needed all the help they could get so I'm looking forward to see how things sort out in the future for them and how Connor and Rose will be. <br /><br />Overall I can't say I loved this book but I'm certainly intrigued and the 3.6 stars are basically for Connor, Rose and everything I liked about this book. Not so much for the main character, I know but hopefully I will enjoy reading about them as the books go.</span>

<div id="review_1346432082" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1346432082" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1346432082?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Pearl by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9810857">✿ سخىة ✿</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=sobfest">sobfest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2015-reads">2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=cute-book-couple">cute-book-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=fake-relationship">fake-relationship</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=fangirling">fangirling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=highly-recommended-na">highly-recommended-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=hot-male-characters">hot-male-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=smexy-read">smexy-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1346432082" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12768577664634851018"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We're terrible at so many things, but the only thing we've always been halfway decent at is being together.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>A New Adult book at its finest! So many feels!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432903ra/870782.gif' width='350' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>To my fabulous friend <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/9810857-scarlett' rel='nofollow noopener'>Scarlett</a> who heartily recommended this book and this series to me, I owe you one, girl! A big thank you! (Check out her beautiful <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1407042270?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>review</a> on this book :)<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22296542.Addicted_to_You__Addicted___1_' title='Addicted to You (Addicted, #1) by Krista Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Addicted to You</a> is definitely a book that made me become literally <b>addicted</b>. As a lover of New Adult genre, I expected myself to feel drawn with this book the mo</span>
  <span id="freeText12768577664634851018" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We're terrible at so many things, but the only thing we've always been halfway decent at is being together.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>A New Adult book at its finest! So many feels!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432903ra/870782.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To my fabulous friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/9810857-scarlett" rel="nofollow noopener">Scarlett</a> who heartily recommended this book and this series to me, I owe you one, girl! A big thank you! (Check out her beautiful <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1407042270?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">review</a> on this book :)<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22296542.Addicted_to_You__Addicted___1_" title="Addicted to You (Addicted, #1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Addicted to You</a> is definitely a book that made me become literally <b>addicted</b>. As a lover of New Adult genre, I expected myself to feel drawn with this book the moment I started it, because well.. it's apparently a guilty-pleasure read. And I'm happy to say that this book is not just about sex. It comes in a very emotional, unique romantic storyline that absolutely tugs the heart. <br><br>This book is a story about <b>Lily Calloway</b> and <b>Loren Hale</b>-- two perfectly flawed characters who are secretly self-conscious about their addiction. Lily, a girl who is addicted to sex, grew up together with her bestfriend and pretend boyfriend Loren a.k.a Lo, who is on the other hand, addicted to alcohol. On the outside, they may look a really perfect couple because of their rich, shiny families, but little did everyone know that they have secrets that they shamefully keep. Thus, they choose to appear perfect and depend on each other to sustain their addiction.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>We may not be good for each other, but sometimes I feel like he's the only guy who could ever love me.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The book definitely gave me a lot of surprises. The characters have this <i>undeniable chemistry</i>. Not to mention that Lo is absolutely one scorching hot male lead. Definitely <b>a new book boyfriend to add on my list</b>. And as the cover suggests, apparently it's one hot and smexy read. But like I said, it's not only about sex-- it's filled with emotionally-driven romance, twists, and drama. I was so surprised to find myself ugly crying with this book, especially at the last parts. The ending was so emotional and a cliffhanger as well.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>And I suppose, the fear of losing each other is always stronger than the pain we cause.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>As a whole, this book is definitely a must-read. I appreciate the message it carries, specifically about accepting the person you love despite the imperfections and holding on to that person until the very end. I also appreciate the way family love was emphasized here. It's a book with a real emotional depth. Officially, it's now <b>my new favorite New Adult book!</b> :)<br><br>Rating:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993136i/16730745.jpg" width="200" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This review is also posted on my blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/2015/10/18/review-addicted-to-you-by-krista-and-becca-ritchie/">https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/201...</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445940227i/16723670.jpg" width="380" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993261i/16730770.jpg" width="200" height="120" alt="bibliopearl" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="12768577664634851018" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3119302695" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3119302695" />
    <a title="Irena BookDustMagic" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17737927-irena-bookdustmagic"><img alt="Irena BookDustMagic" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1362943196p2/17737927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3119302695?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Irena BookDustMagic" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Irena BookDustMagic" href="/user/show/17737927-irena-bookdustmagic">Irena BookDustMagic</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3119302695" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6274597415065442222">Addicted to You is a novel that was recommended to me back in the day when NA was HUGE.<br/>It's free on Kindle, so I download it immediately, but then as I started to explore the genre I decided it was not for me, so this romance stayed on hold for years.<br/><br/>At the beginning of this year I found myself in the mood to pick it up, so I did.<br/><br/>Since the main protagonist is addicted to sex, and the main male character to alcohol, I expected lots of graphic scenes and steamy moments, but instead, to my pleasant</span>
  <span id="freeText6274597415065442222" style="display:none">Addicted to You is a novel that was recommended to me back in the day when NA was HUGE.<br />It's free on Kindle, so I download it immediately, but then as I started to explore the genre I decided it was not for me, so this romance stayed on hold for years.<br /><br />At the beginning of this year I found myself in the mood to pick it up, so I did.<br /><br />Since the main protagonist is addicted to sex, and the main male character to alcohol, I expected lots of graphic scenes and steamy moments, but instead, to my pleasant surprise, I got a well written story without explicit content, but with great message that was not pushed too hard in reader's face.<br /><br />Now I wish I gave this book a chance sooner, to change my mind about NA genre, because it proves there are great books among it.<br />However, I have to stress out that now I'm five years older then I was back in the day, so I like to consider myself wiser and more open minded, so maybe I just wasn't ready for it in 2013 (don't try to correct my math, I can see it's actually 7 years but I like to believe that I age slower).<br /><br />The story is written in first person, which is my favourite way to follow along.<br /><br />I've heard amazing thins about books written by these authors, and now I understand why.<br />I will definitely read more of their work in hope my feelings about their work will stay the same, if not even get better.<br />I already have Kiss the Sky on my Kindle, and also Amor Amor (forgive me if I misspelled it) is high on my wish list.<br /><br />I definitely recommend this novel to romance lovers, especially because it is a freebie.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6274597415065442222" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1146725298" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1146725298" />
    <a title="Lucia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia"><img alt="Lucia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484242793p2/8837962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1146725298?book_show_action=true">Dec 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucia" href="/user/show/8837962-lucia">Lucia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Lucia by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3887412-lisa-lifeinlit">Lisa (lifeinlit)</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8837962-lucia?shelf=5-stars-read">5-stars-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146725298" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer48494518955969248"><b>UPDATE JUNE 2016:</b><br/>Re-reading this series got me emotional all over again. I LOVE Lily's and Lo's story so much!<br/><br/><u>
  <b>SERIES RATING AND SPOILER-FREE REVIEW:</b>
</u><br/><blockquote>Book 1: Addicted To You - 5 STARS<br/>Book 1.5: Ricochet - 4 STARS<br/>Book 2: Addicted For Now - 5 STARS<br/>Book 2.5: Thrive - 4 STARS<br/>Book 3: Addicted After All - 5 STARS </blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423145455i/13591680.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Two addictions, one big lie. In order to keep in good graces of their wealthy parents (and to keep access to trust funds) Lo and Lily had to hide their addictions and pretend to be together.</span>
  <span id="freeText48494518955969248" style="display:none"><b>UPDATE JUNE 2016:</b><br>Re-reading this series got me emotional all over again. I LOVE Lily's and Lo's story so much!<br><br><u>
  <b>SERIES RATING AND SPOILER-FREE REVIEW:</b>
</u><br><blockquote>Book 1: Addicted To You - 5 STARS<br>Book 1.5: Ricochet - 4 STARS<br>Book 2: Addicted For Now - 5 STARS<br>Book 2.5: Thrive - 4 STARS<br>Book 3: Addicted After All - 5 STARS </blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423145455i/13591680.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Two addictions, one big lie. In order to keep in good graces of their wealthy parents (and to keep access to trust funds) Lo and Lily had to hide their addictions and pretend to be together. The truth about his alcoholism and her sexual escapades could not only ruin reputations of their families but also take away their freedom of supporting their addictions. But how long can they keep the charade?<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"We’re in a three year long fake relationship. We live together. He’s heard me orgasm from one room over. I’ve seen him sleep in his own puke. And even though our parents believe we’re one small step from engagement, we’ll never have sex again."</i>
</blockquote><br>Who wouldn’t be intrigued after such a start? I was utterly fascinated by the premise of this series and I was curious how (and if) Lily and Lo would be able to develop something more than friendship considering their life styles. For years, they were enabling each other’s addictions. But when their feelings get out of hand, how will Lo deals with Lily’s sex drive being out of control? What will Lily think of Lo being drunk all the time? Can she be monogamous and not be ruled by her need for orgasms? Will they ever be able to do a 180° turn-around and do the hard thing and say no to their addictions? Can such two people ever have healthy relationship together? How can they fight their addictions without attracting attention of their families and society? Let me tell you, I was so worked up, needing to find answers to those questions that I literally couldn’t put first three books down. I was prepared for angsty realistic intense ride, but reality of this series was even more all-consuming. I was looking for unforgettable emotional contemporary tale and got exactly that (and much more).<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I want to love you more than I love this" - he waves his bottle - "and I don’t know how else to do it unless there’s something to lose."</i>
</blockquote><br>Addicted series is not the easiest read. Some parts were angsty and sad, others truly dangerous and nasty. Addiction, in whatever form, is never pretty. And in this series it shows its very ugly side. It was so heartbreaking to see to what lengths would some people go to support their addictions. And I’m not sure if it is masochist in me talking, but this intense angst was exactly what made these books so special for me and what distinguish them from all others NA novels out there.<br><br>But don’t worry, this series is not only full of despair. It is also about power of true love, about strength of family ties and friendships. It is story about learning to accept help and about learning to love yourself even with all your flaws. I fell in love not only with Lily and Lo, but also with all side characters who made me laugh a lot and helped to balance this tale so it wouldn’t turn into completely depressive read.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423145455i/13591681.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How to sum up this series? Heartbreaking and soul-crashing but simultaneously beautiful and entertaining modern family drama. Lily &amp; Lo’s story touched my heart. They may be flawed but oh so very real and dear to me. These messed up (but unique) characters became special to me and this series will stay with me forever. I highly recommend Addicted series to those who are looking for intense and memorable NA novels!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"The parts of me that I love the most are the parts that belong to her."</i>
</blockquote><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Reading Is My Breathing</b>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="48494518955969248" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="L A i N E Y" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y"><img alt="L A i N E Y" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546138360p2/10752235.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1593814740?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="L A i N E Y" class="user" itemprop="url" name="L A i N E Y" href="/user/show/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y">L A i N E Y</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y?shelf=ooh-chemistry">ooh-chemistry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y?shelf=blurb-perfect">blurb-perfect</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y?shelf=na">na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y?shelf=angst-galore">angst-galore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y?shelf=reread">reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10752235-l-a-i-n-e-y?shelf=this-ship-will-sink-me">this-ship-will-sink-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1593814740" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13865215405012073804">Two years almost to the day and a reread later, Addicted to You still delivered what I loved from before: smoking chemistry and glorious angst. <br/><br/>I always say this is the best NA book/series I have read and that still holds very true second time around. Indeed I think it’s even more true, in a sense. I’m so glad I reread this because I just cannot fathom why <i>why</i> I gave this only 4 stars?? I must have been mad! <br/><br/>Well, already amended.<br/><br/>My preparation is complete. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22296819.Addicted_for_Now__Addicted___2_' title='Addicted for Now (Addicted, #2) by Krista Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Addicted for Now</a>, I’m ready for you!<br/><br/><br/><br/><i>——</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13865215405012073804" style="display:none">Two years almost to the day and a reread later, Addicted to You still delivered what I loved from before: smoking chemistry and glorious angst. <br /><br />I always say this is the best NA book/series I have read and that still holds very true second time around. Indeed I think it’s even more true, in a sense. I’m so glad I reread this because I just cannot fathom why <i>why</i> I gave this only 4 stars?? I must have been mad! <br /><br />Well, already amended.<br /><br />My preparation is complete. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22296819.Addicted_for_Now__Addicted___2_" title="Addicted for Now (Addicted, #2) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Addicted for Now</a>, I’m ready for you!<br /><br /><br /><br /><i>——— original review ———</i><br /><br /><br />Hey, actually quite good!<br /><br />This was the first New Adult novel I came across that didn't annoy me with stupid dialogue but I'm fairly new for this genre so maybe I've been out of luck before(?) If that's the case I'm glad it veered in the right direction with this. <br /><br />I do like these characters. Love to see them again.<br /><br />Can't speak in terms of how it handled the addiction issues though since I am pretty ignorant on that. But, generally speaking, the story was interesting enough for me to keep reading and i will be picking up the next one.<br /><br />Curious to see how Lo's doing, mostly. But secondary characters are pretty interesting too so that is always a huge plus.<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>rating: ★★★★½</b><br /><br /></span>

Just no. I know this was supposed to really hit the old emotions, but for me????<br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/illinois/chicago/" rel="nofollow noopener">

    <a title="Mysza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza"><img alt="Mysza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433922560p2/14262653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1482092820?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mysza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mysza" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza">Mysza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14262653-mysza?shelf=favorite-read">favorite-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1482092820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15677725871496612603">I didn't initially review this book but I am currently now on book 3 and I am becoming "addicted" to this series. And damn, if those books don't deserve a review than I don't know what does. <br/><br/>I didn't love this one but I liked it. I was a little sceptical after finishing it but I am so glad I continued with the series because it's just getting better and better. And if you are too on the fence whether to continue, please do, I promise you won't regret.<br/><br/>Lily and Lo... she's a sex addict, he's an al</span>
  <span id="freeText15677725871496612603" style="display:none">I didn't initially review this book but I am currently now on book 3 and I am becoming "addicted" to this series. And damn, if those books don't deserve a review than I don't know what does. <br><br>I didn't love this one but I liked it. I was a little sceptical after finishing it but I am so glad I continued with the series because it's just getting better and better. And if you are too on the fence whether to continue, please do, I promise you won't regret.<br><br>Lily and Lo... she's a sex addict, he's an alcoholic. Such a strange duo, both trying to look as this perfect couple and at the same time enabling and hiding their addictions from the world outside their bubble. But how long can you destroy yourself and the person you love before it all explodes?<blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I love you, but I want to love you enough that I never choose alcohol over you. Not even for a moment. I want to be someone you deserve.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>That was a really good start to LiLo's epic love story. To be continued....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452498755ra/17699144.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15677725871496612603" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3944703772668212499">Thanks to everyone who participated in the blog tour. And double thanks if you've read (and hopefully enjoyed) <i>Addicted to You</i>. We're so excited to share the rest of the series! Look out for Ricochet (Addicted #1.5) on August 1st, 2013. Trust me, you're going to want to read it if you liked this one ;) <br/><br/><b>TEASER POSTER</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401299111i/9782649._SY540_.jpg' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>UPDATE: Almost 1 year later</b> <br/>It's pretty much insane that this series is still going strong, and it's hard to believe this was our debut together. I just want to thank everyone again f</span>
  <span id="freeText3944703772668212499" style="display:none">Thanks to everyone who participated in the blog tour. And double thanks if you've read (and hopefully enjoyed) <i>Addicted to You</i>. We're so excited to share the rest of the series! Look out for Ricochet (Addicted #1.5) on August 1st, 2013. Trust me, you're going to want to read it if you liked this one ;) <br><br><b>TEASER POSTER</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1401299111i/9782649._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>UPDATE: Almost 1 year later</b> <br>It's pretty much insane that this series is still going strong, and it's hard to believe this was our debut together. I just want to thank everyone again for giving Lily &amp; Lo a chance. Their final books are going to be released June and late this summer of 2014. It's been one amazing journey, and we're so happy that so many of you have taken it with us :)</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3426617711143764128">3.5 Stars<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388359966i/7809829.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"We're in a three-year long fake relationship. We live together. He's heard me orgasm one room over. I've seen him sleep in his own puke....."</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388359966i/7809830._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book offers an unusual and interesting scenario with Lily and Lo. Two friends from wealthy families living with their addiction demons. Anonymous sex is what she likes, what she craves.... He craves the bottle..... Their world scares me, their story had me on tenterhooks at times and had amazing scope for angst and drama.... <br/><br/>During the ea</span>
  <span id="freeText3426617711143764128" style="display:none">3.5 Stars<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388359966i/7809829.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"We're in a three-year long fake relationship. We live together. He's heard me orgasm one room over. I've seen him sleep in his own puke....."</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388359966i/7809830._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book offers an unusual and interesting scenario with Lily and Lo. Two friends from wealthy families living with their addiction demons. Anonymous sex is what she likes, what she craves.... He craves the bottle..... Their world scares me, their story had me on tenterhooks at times and had amazing scope for angst and drama.... <br><br>During the early stages of the story, the characters kept making my heart skip a beat. The possibilities of their relationship, every time they spoke to each other.... And their inner thoughts....<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"The way he watches me with rapt attention sets my whole body aflame."<br><br>"His smile widens, filling up his face into something beautiful."</b>
</blockquote><br>Lo especially made me swoon but I felt it didn't deliver as I anticipated all the way through. <i>I was waiting for magic....</i><br><br><u>
  <i>And I wished for more....</i>
</u><br>Some parts of the story I found a little hard to believe....<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b> “You’ve been waiting around for six years……. Six years of miss-communication.” </b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Really??? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ 6 years of miss-communication????  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I could see where the story was going; I would have liked more surprises and twists along the way.....<br><br>I would have enjoyed a slightly faster paced story but the authors were giving care and attention to the subject so maybe it had to be this way???<br><br><i>
  <u>I Loved </u>
</i><br><i>The.... Will they/won't they get it together....??? Will either of them say how they really feel???</i> This part of the story was very beautiful, their journey touching...... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388406017i/7826760.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>“I didn’t think I was hurting anyone but me.” </b>
</blockquote><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>"I'm here for you. Always." ~ Lo</b>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><i> Just beautiful, but is it true???</i><br><br>Addiction affects everyone who loves you, but what happens when..... <br><i> People with an addiction love each other??? Can they truly love each other???</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I’ve protected him. From everyone but himself."</b>
</blockquote><br>We see glimpses of why they may be the way they are..... Are they the products of their upbringing??? The nature versus nurture argument always fascinates me and this story made me think about that....<br><br>All in all, I liked the story and the characters, especially, Lo. I LOVED their tangible connection to each other, but, for me, this story was a little slow in places, I could easily have taken more angst and drama and more skipped heart beats.<i> I needed more heart flutters.</i> I felt like I was always on the edge of something amazing which leads me to the conclusion that I should definitely follow the story of Lily and Lo. <b>Certainly friends reviews indicate that I'm on the edge of greatness with this series. So a little break and I will get back to Lily and Lo.</b> <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>“Wait for me.”<br>“ I need you to wait for me.” </b>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>
  <b>If you've been looking at this story and wondering??? Pick it up and give it a read you may find yourself on an amazing journey!!! </b>
</i><br><br><br><br>♥ Br with the gorgeous Barb &amp; Deanna<br><br><br>***Arc provided by NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
