<div id="review_720876242" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/720876242" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/720876242?book_show_action=true">Sep 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18369048-addicted-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=netgalley-edelweiss">netgalley-edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=6-stars-of-brilliance">6-stars-of-brilliance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=plain-jane-lovin">plain-jane-lovin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=dark-taboo-forbidden-reads">dark-taboo-forbidden-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=drop-everything-and-read-it-now">drop-everything-and-read-it-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer720876242" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer84094561793786210"><b>6 GLOWING STARS!!! </b><br/><br/>Wow, what a HOT mess! I need to be upfront and say, this book has all the ingredients for an immediate DNF from me, yet I LOVED it! Maybe it was because of all the disappointing books I read before and this one broke my book slump? I don’t know, but the first thing that I thought of once I finished was <b>this book reminded me why I read NA romance </b>. <br/><br/>So this story is about Lily and Loren, one a sex addict and the other an alcoholic O_O Right from the beginning, I felt like this b</span>
  <span id="freeText84094561793786210" style="display:none"><b>6 GLOWING STARS!!! </b><br /><br />Wow, what a HOT mess! I need to be upfront and say, this book has all the ingredients for an immediate DNF from me, yet I LOVED it! Maybe it was because of all the disappointing books I read before and this one broke my book slump? I don’t know, but the first thing that I thought of once I finished was <b>this book reminded me why I read NA romance </b>. <br /><br />So this story is about Lily and Loren, one a sex addict and the other an alcoholic O_O Right from the beginning, I felt like this book would be different from other NA reads, since it isn’t just the hero or the heroine who needs saving, it’s both, so how could a romance work out? And both addictions to sex and alcohol are extremely hard to overcome, and even more difficult to portray, but K&amp;B did a fantastic job of convincing me, the reader, the hopelessness of their situation, their unshakable addictions, and later, their very <i>real</i> struggle against these addictions. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“I don’t want to be fixed. I just want to live and feed my appetite. It just so happens that my appetite is a sexual one.”</b>
</i><br /><br />In all outwardly appearances, Lily seems to be a quiet and reserved person, but she really is a sex addict. From a young age, she’s had a looooooooong history of sexual activity, and to her, it’s not so much she’s addicted to the sex itself, it’s more she’s addicted to the <i>high</i>, the feeling of empowerment she gets when she’s sexing it up in bathroom stalls, backseats of cars, bar corners, and basically <i>anywhere</i> and <i>everywhere</i>. Her one saving grace, the one person who is her rock, is her childhood best friend Loren. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“His addiction scares me sometimes. Alcoholism can destroy livers and kidneys, and one day, he may not wake up from a night of bingeing. But how can I tell him to stop?”</b>
</i><br /><br />Loren “Lo” drinks himself into a stupor daily. His reasons aren’t revealed until later in the story, but as I was reading, I could <b>
  <i>feel</i>
</b> how jagged his pain was, even though I didn’t know where it stemmed from. I connected with his character so strongly, I think if I could, I would be able to reach into the book and physically touch his pain. I thought Lil's struggles were heartbreaking, but when I got to the core of Lo's emotions, my heart cracked. <br /><br />This is no sweet, vanilla romance. In my opinion, it’s dark, it’s raw, it’s broken. Their addictions are so ingrained that in order to be together, they have to fight <i>themselves</i>, constantly, daily, and to see them succeed...and fail, sometimes got too emotional for me to read. That being said, this book also has the most EPIC banter between the characters, and I swear I probably woke up my entire apartment complex with my laughing! ^_^ To read a book that triggers both extreme ends of my emotional scale is truly a phenomenally written story. <br /><br />The ending of this book left me feeling open and vulnerable. There isn’t a cliffhanger, but there are literally so many routes Lo and Lil’s story could go, and my biggest fear is that the route they take will end up with their separation. I, for one, cannot wait to start reading the next books in the series! As soon as I can kick real life out of the house, I will be cuddled up with book 1.5 and reading away! <br /><br /><u>Note to all my wonderful GR friends:</u> if you do choose to read this series (and I hope you do), PLEASE don’t give up on Lil and Lo. I know they will try your patience dearly, and you all know how impatient and hot-headed I am. I promise it will be a satisfying read!<br /><br />I originally intended to give this book the full 5 stars, however, the unique premise of the book, the detailed, poignant portrayal of these characters, and the fact it broke my book slump, makes this a 6 star read for me! <br /><br /><i>ARC kindly provided by publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="84094561793786210" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_756018324" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/756018324" />
    <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs"><img alt="Amy | Foxy Blogs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366176904p2/9955253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/756018324?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18369048-addicted-to-you">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Amy | Foxy Blogs by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4017258-aishah">Aishah </a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=february-2014">february-2014</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2014-books">2014-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer756018324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14792192574131515875"><b>FREE</b><br/>#1 <b>Addicted To You</b> ➜ <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1jXupa5'>http://amzn.to/1jXupa5</a><br/>2/12/2015<br/>***************************<br/><br/>**3.5 Addicted stars**<br/><br/><b>ADDICTED TO YOU</b> centers around two broken people each enabling the other. <b>Lily</b> is addicted to sex while her boyfriend, <b>Lo</b>, is addicted to alcohol. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Sex on a bar. It'd be like our addictions making love.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>As a society we all know what an alcoholic is but do we know what a sex addict is? A sex addict is someone who has a compulsion towards sexual thoughts and acts. Like all addictions,</span>
  <span id="freeText14792192574131515875" style="display:none"><b>FREE</b><br />#1 <b>Addicted To You</b> ➜ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1jXupa5">http://amzn.to/1jXupa5</a><br />2/12/2015<br />***************************<br /><br />**3.5 Addicted stars**<br /><br /><b>ADDICTED TO YOU</b> centers around two broken people each enabling the other. <b>Lily</b> is addicted to sex while her boyfriend, <b>Lo</b>, is addicted to alcohol. <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Sex on a bar. It'd be like our addictions making love.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>As a society we all know what an alcoholic is but do we know what a sex addict is? A sex addict is someone who has a compulsion towards sexual thoughts and acts. Like all addictions, its negative impact on the addict and on family members increases as the disorder progresses. <b>
  <i>"It's not something that people can easily accept or understand."</i>
</b><br /><br />For the first 40% of the book I was very unsure how I felt. I wasn't connecting with all the impersonal sex. But I started to enjoy the story more when the secondary characters were introduced. <br /><br />Let's meet these secondary characters:<br /><b>1) Connor</b> - Wow, he could be such a pretentious jerk but I really liked him. I felt he really cared for Lily and Lo and wanted to be their friend. <b>
  <i>"You two are so weird." Being called weird by Connor is like a unicorn calling a horse magical. It makes no damn sense, which is why Lo and I break into smiles...</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>2) Ryke</b> - I had him figured out right from the start. What he was trying to do and who he is makes me look forward to reading his spin-off. <br /><br />By the end of the book I started thinking about what will happen in the next book. Even though this book was ★ ★ ★ I plan to continue on because I need to make sure these two turn out okay.<br /><b><br />*********************************************************</b><br />Addicted series is interconnected with two spin-offs. The authors have written the books in 3 “phases”. Each phase is a complete story line with a satisfying enough conclusion. <br /><br /><u>Recommended reading order:</u><br /><b>PHASE 1 (Lily &amp; Lo): </b><br />{#1} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18369048.Addicted_to_You__Addicted___1_" title="Addicted to You (Addicted, #1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Addicted to You</a> | {#1.5} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/19545617.Ricochet__Addicted___1_5_" title="Ricochet (Addicted, #1.5) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Ricochet</a> | {#2} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17969317.Addicted_for_Now__Addicted___2_" title="Addicted for Now (Addicted, #2) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Addicted for Now</a><br /><br /><b>PHASE 2 (Rose and Connor) | (Daisy &amp; Ryke):</b><br />{spin-off} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18308262.Kiss_the_Sky__Calloway_Sisters___1__Addicted___2_1_" title="Kiss the Sky (Calloway Sisters, #1; Addicted, #2.1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss the Sky</a> | {spin-off} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18308266.Hothouse_Flower__Calloway_Sisters___2__Addicted___2_2_" title="Hothouse Flower (Calloway Sisters, #2; Addicted, #2.2) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Hothouse Flower</a> <br /><br /><b>PHASE 3 (Lily &amp; Lo):</b><br />{#2.5} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18479451.Thrive__Addicted___2_5_" title="Thrive (Addicted, #2.5) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Thrive</a> | {#3} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18308270.Addicted_After_All__Addicted___3_" title="Addicted After All (Addicted, #3) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Addicted After All</a><br /><br /><b>PHASE 4 (Rose and Connor) | (Daisy &amp; Ryke):</b><br />{spin-off} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22024901.Fuel_the_Fire__Calloway_Sisters___3__Addicted___3_1_" title="Fuel the Fire (Calloway Sisters, #3; Addicted, #3.1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Fuel the Fire</a> | {spin-off} <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22024907.Long_Way_Down__Calloway_Sisters___4__Addicted___3_2_" title="Long Way Down (Calloway Sisters, #4; Addicted, #3.2) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Long Way Down</a><br /></span>

  <span id="freeText6298385763140644924" style="display:none"><br><b>*4.5 addictive, soulwrenching, heartwarming STARS*.</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385061872i/7059340._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385061872i/7059341._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>An intense, powerful, emotional, original and captivating read that had me hooked from the first page! I absolutely loved the main characters as well as the supporting cast. Lo and Lily both had their issues, they weren't perfect, but that's what made them all the more appealing and interesting to read about. <br><br>This was the first time I'd read a book about someone with a sex addiction and it was fascinating to experience life through the eyes of someone like Lily. It's not a topic that you come across often and the authors did a fantastic job at creating a realistic story that both makes you sad and gives you hope for the future.<br><br>A highly recommended read!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385062262i/7059399.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>**Copy courtesy of Independent Book Publishers Association, via Netgalley, in exchange for an honest review**</i></span>

  <span id="freeText10991821188067881115" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE -mature content reader discretion advised<br>4 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br><b>FULL REVIEW POSTED 12/28/13</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388205386i/7765656.jpg" alt=" photo AddictedtoYoupic_zps7edf3068.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Fuckity FUCK FUCK FUCK, I just…..FUCK. Pardon my language but this book left my mind whirling. Lily and her sex addiction…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388251456ra/7779068.gif" alt=" photo wowgif_zpse1d062a5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Addicted to you is about two friends, Lily and Loren, they’re in a fake relationship with one another to help cover the tracks of their addictions. Lily’s addiction is sex and Lo’s addiction is alcohol. Both are heading down a destructive path and neither one can stop the other from the destruction that is sure to come.<br><br>Eventually what was just for show becomes the real deal. Lily and Lo make it official and things become a bigger tangled mess with them both feeding each others addictions. And it was scary. <br><br>Alright bare with me I'm severely behind on reviews but I want to say a few things about this book. Here is the deal I liked it. I did not exactly love it. First, I struggled on whether or not to give it 4 stars but in the end I did, mainly because of the story's impact and the undeniable writing that sucks you in. <br><br>You have these two people struggling to hide their addictions from friends and family but.. Wait pause, correction they do not have friends, their addictions prevent that. Now back to what I was saying, even though neither addiction managed to out shine the other for some reason I struggled with Lily's sex addiction.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388251456i/7779069.jpg" alt=" photo addictedtoyoucollagepic_zps0d80f017.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't think I truly grasped how out of control she was until the fashion show scene. Crazy, I know, especially with all her sexcapades. But ummm…that whole scene after the show was so….<b>embarrassing</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388251456ra/7779070.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mj0ogaTS6k1ryu3g1o1_500_zps717a9ffa.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I kind of felt like a deer caught in the headlights and for me, that was my shi*t just got real moment with Lily’s character.<br><br> To be honest it was hard to read about their constant denial, co dependency and the insufferable way they enabled one another. It was quite sad but I think that was what drove the point of addiction home.<br> Nothing about it is fun, easy or to be taken lightly. Bravo to Krista and Becca Ritchie for that!Thank goodness for Ryke. Ryke saw through the BS facades Lily ad Lo had going on. And yeah I know it’s a bit more to it than that but I prefer not to dive in to that story line.<br><br> The one thing I really enjoyed was the fact that this book had some great comedic scenes and lines that pretty much had me burst in to laughter. Her on her laptop in class..PRICELESS! I laughed hysterically.<br><br><b>
  <u>My Sweet and Sour</u>
</b><br><b>My Sweet-</b> What Lo said to Lily at the end… It’s spoilerish so you would have to read the book to actually know what I am referring to. **Hand to heart** <b>So S W E E T!!!!</b><br><b> My Sour-</b> The way that addiction<b> ruled</b> their lives. Very hard to read, yet so true to life.<br><br><u>My Rating and Why</u><br>I gave Addicted to You 4 STARS for its unique story line and its portrayal of two people using each other to hide their addiction. No denying that the story pulls you right in which is a nod to good writing. Well done to Krista and Becca Ritchie!<br><br><u>My Ratings</u><br><b>Characters-</b> Complicated with an excellent cast of secondary characters<br><b>Writing Style-</b> The writing was good, the pulls you in and spits you out<b> G O O D</b><br><b>Plot/Storyline-</b> Two people using one another as a crutch to hide their addictions both are in a downward spiral<br><b>Steam Factor-</b> Medium/Moderately Steamy<br><b>Overall-</b> I enjoyed it! And I plan to continue the series!<br><b>My Recommendation:</b> Check it out, it’s worth the read!<br><b><br><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br><b>For more reviews got to:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">www.realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot...</a> <br><b>Like us on Facebook:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/realitybitesletsgetlost">www.facebook.com/realitybitesletsgetlost</a><br></span>

<div id="review_962593491" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/962593491" />
    <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time"><img alt="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460037460p2/9072385.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/962593491?book_show_action=true">Jun 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" class="user" itemprop="url" name="*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time" href="/user/show/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time">*J* Too Many Books Too Little Time</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=liked-a-lot">liked-a-lot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=tums-required">tums-required</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9072385-j-too-many-books-too-little-time?shelf=happy-for-now-ending">happy-for-now-ending</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer962593491" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1865247806662275606">4.5--<b>Addicted</b>--Stars!!<br/><br/>I really dragged ass on this series. I don't normally like to read multi-book series about the same MCs. But with that being said, I am really glad I finally gave this one a go. <br/><br/>It was a bit too angsty for my liking. But I've been assured that there is less angst in the remainging books in the series. Thank goodness because <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404161704ra/10200554.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Adicted to You is the story of two childhood friends. Two people who found solace in each other. Two people with <b>addictions</b> that used each other to hide</span>
  <span id="freeText1865247806662275606" style="display:none">4.5--<b>Addicted</b>--Stars!!<br><br>I really dragged ass on this series. I don't normally like to read multi-book series about the same MCs. But with that being said, I am really glad I finally gave this one a go. <br><br>It was a bit too angsty for my liking. But I've been assured that there is less angst in the remainging books in the series. Thank goodness because <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404161704ra/10200554.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Adicted to You is the story of two childhood friends. Two people who found solace in each other. Two people with <b>addictions</b> that used each other to hide them. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"We’re in a three-year long fake relationship. We live together. He’s heard me orgasm from one room over. I’ve seen him sleep in his own puke."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><b>Lily:</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1399344641ra/9538118.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I didn't just have sex for fun or because it made me feel empowered. I liked the high, the rush, and how it seemed to fill an emptiness that kept growing inside of me."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>I had a hard time understanding Lily's sex addiction. That doesn't mean it isn't real. There were times she literally could not function until she fulfilled that need....no matter when or where she was. <br><br><b>Loren (Lo):</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404161704ra/10200555.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The alcoholic. The functioning alcoholic. Lo spends his days drinking. Sometimes blacking out. His days are a haze of whiskey, bourbon, rum. <br><br>Honestly, these two....were just wow! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404161704ra/10200556.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Our selfishness wedges between us. Neither of us is willing to give up what we love for each other."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"...the fear of losing each other is always stronger than the pain we cause."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>It was brutal to read about both Lily and Lo's addictions. Painful to watch Lily give herself so freely to anyone, everyone. For Lo to drink his life away. To care more about his next drink, then his own well-being, more than Lily at times. <br><br>But it's all a facade. An act. A part in a play. They pretend to be what they need to be, to keep their secrets hidden. Depending on each other, needing each other. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I need him more than he needs me. His vice is a bottle of whiskey. Mine is his body. So when we fight, I’m the one who loses out in the end."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400918324ra/9737712.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lily craves Lo in ways that she shouldn't. And Lo's just waiting for Lily to ask him for she needs. What he wants to give her. <br><br>They've only ever had each other. No friends. They keep their family at a distance to protect their secrets. <br><br>A family trip forces Lo and Lily's relationship to change. They are both finally honest with how they feel about each other. Maybe not having to pretend will make things easier. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“We may not be good for each other, but sometimes I feel like he’s the only guy who could ever love me.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Being with Lo, means Lily relies on him to feed her addiction. If he can't satisfy her needs, she would have to find someone else who can. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386532042ra/7385338.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lo and Lily actually make some friends. But letting friends in, means the possibility of letting their secrets out. While Lily's addiction is easier to hide, Lo's isn't. Deep down Lily wants nothing more than for Lo to not need the booze. For her to be enough to make Lo quit. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I want to love you more than I love this”—he waves his bottle—“and I don’t know how else to do it unless there’s something to lose.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Their addictions constantly weigh them down. At times too much for them both to bear. But there's no way out. How do you save someone that doesn't want to be saved? For Lo and Lily, they may not have a choice.... <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I'll always be yours. No distance or time apart will change that, Lily.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1865247806662275606" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_661928671" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/661928671" />
    <a title="Glass" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4808910-glass"><img alt="Glass" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583244629p2/4808910.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/661928671?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Glass" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Glass" href="/user/show/4808910-glass">Glass</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17830264-addicted-to-you">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Glass by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/7399193-siiri-little-pieces-of-imagination">Siiri (Little Pieces of Imagination)</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=fangirling-like-crazy">fangirling-like-crazy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=girl-power">girl-power</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=way-too-hot">way-too-hot</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer661928671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5861494497666042939"> I am not a stubborn person. <i>*crickets*</i> Well, sometimes I am not. <i>*more crickets*</i> Okay, I am always subborn. But also I know when to admit that I was wrong. <i>*cri..*</i> Shut up! I admit it - I. Was. Wrong. Can we move on, please?<br/><br/> Okay, where was I? Loren Hale and Lily Calloway. That twin sisters who started off as bloggers and turned into brilliant authors. My new adult addiction. Siiri from <a href='http://littlepiecesofimagination.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Little Pieces of Imagination</a> made me read this. (Check out <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/594580692?book_show_action=false&page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>her review</a>, too.) But seriously, I cannot believe </span>
  <span id="freeText5861494497666042939" style="display:none"> I am not a stubborn person. <i>*crickets*</i> Well, sometimes I am not. <i>*more crickets*</i> Okay, I am always subborn. But also I know when to admit that I was wrong. <i>*cri..*</i> Shut up! I admit it - I. Was. Wrong. Can we move on, please?<br /><br /> Okay, where was I? Loren Hale and Lily Calloway. That twin sisters who started off as bloggers and turned into brilliant authors. My new adult addiction. Siiri from <a href="http://littlepiecesofimagination.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Little Pieces of Imagination</a> made me read this. (Check out <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/594580692?book_show_action=false&amp;page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">her review</a>, too.) But seriously, I cannot believe that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/605849760?book_show_action=false&amp;page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Tanja read Addicted to You</a> before me - she is not new adult fan. And she read it before me.<br /> It took only a little bit over a year for our Estonian friend Siiri to finally persuade me to read Addicted series. Main reason for my reluctance was all the hype and the the fact that I had really bad experiences in the past with new adult recommendations. Only thing that I can say is that I am glad that I have waited until now because I can binge-read and not go crazy while waiting for a new sequel.<br /><br /><blockquote>Glass has officially turned into one of those shippers or OTP fangirls.<br /><i>(however it's called)</i></blockquote><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Why I loved Addicted to You?</u>
</b><br /><br /> <b>Original idea.</b> The most usual stereotype of NA novels is a good, overly naive, girl (who is usually a virgin), and I am not fan of those. So imagine my surprise when I realized that main female character is a sex addict. Yes, I know - addiction is a bad thing, but lets focus here on the part where female sexuality is something that Addicted to You is mostly about. Not the million times seen "I have no luck when it comes to sex, but this one special, alpha male makes me act like a porn star" scenario. Lily is like any other human being - male or female - with sexual and other primal urges we all share. Yes, she has a problem, but her sexual identity is not determined trough her relationship status.<br /><br /> <b>Angst.</b> Oh, sweet, sweet Aphrodite, this was torture to read sometimes. Not the bad thing - Krista and Becca Ritchie managed to pull you into the roller-coaster called Lo &amp; Lily without all I-love-him-but-I-hate-her issues. (Am I the only one who noticed how we usually hate female characters, but love all the guys in NA novels?)<br /> <br /> <b>Writing.</b> Just perfect.<br /><br /> <b>Lily, Lo, Ryke, Connor, Rose...</b> With every new chapter, I change my answer to the question: Who is your favorite character? This is one of those rare books where I love them all.<br /><br /><br /> <b>Final judgement?</b> Darker read, but still pretty tame considering a topic. Perfect for fans of new adult who want something a little bit different. Definitely only for those over 18. Yes, it has drama and modern fairy tale feel, but that is something that works perfectly when it comes to Addicted to You. <br /><br /><b>Review posted at <a href="http://jacitamati.blogspot.com/2014/12/addicted-to-you-by-krista-and-becca.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Ja čitam, a ti?</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="5861494497666042939" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/755440106?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18369048-addicted-to-you">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=arc-copy-net-galley">arc-copy-net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=november-reads">november-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer755440106" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12741308107533115957"><br/>This is not your traditional "lovey dovey" romance book. This story is about a couple who battle with addiction in their daily lives. It is dark,raw,unsettling,ugly; but most importantly it is honest and very realistic. Addiction is not pretty, nor is it fun. Lily and Loren have grown up together, and from a very young age they have learned to enable one another and share each others secrets. This is their story, and it is unlike anything I have ever read before. I applaud the author for writing</span>
  <span id="freeText12741308107533115957" style="display:none"><br />This is not your traditional "lovey dovey" romance book. This story is about a couple who battle with addiction in their daily lives. It is dark,raw,unsettling,ugly; but most importantly it is honest and very realistic. Addiction is not pretty, nor is it fun. Lily and Loren have grown up together, and from a very young age they have learned to enable one another and share each others secrets. This is their story, and it is unlike anything I have ever read before. I applaud the author for writing a story that is unconventional and could be looked upon as controversial. Having had addiction touch my own life through my family, I can honestly say that this is a very accurate description of what living with addiction is like. Also, it doesn't just affect the person who is addicted; but the family as a whole. I found this story to be extremely powerful, and it broke my heart to watch as Lily and Lo isolated themselves from their loved ones just so they could continue on in their sickness. You see, that is what addiction really is; a sickness.<br /><br />Lily and Lo have been going to college and living together for three years. Their families are under the assumption that they have been in a love relationship for that amount of time as well. In actual fact, they each have a secret that they both protect one another from revealing to anyone else. Lily is a sex addict, and Lo is living with alcoholism. They enable each other to the point where they can justify their sickness, and feel ok with the fact that they do lie to their family. They also isolate themselves from everyone, as this makes it that much easier to live a lie. As they continue on living in their dysfunction, Lily and Lo's feelings for one another deepen and they fall in love. When they decide to take their relationship to a monogamous one, the biggest question is: Will Lily be able to control her sex addiction enough to stay faithful to Lo? <br />As their relationship continues things slowly start to get out of hand, and they also surprisingly gain a few friends. Connor and Ryke are two guys that develop an interest in Lo and Lily; but in having friends around, the foundation that Lily and Lo have constructed begins to fall apart. Questions start being asked, and their friends begin to notice that not everything is what it appears on the surface. What will happen if their secrets come out? Will Lily and Lo ever conquer their addiction? Or will they continue to enable one another, and choose to stay in what is familiar to them?<br /><br />I did love this book, but I will be honest and say that is was not an easy book to read. It certainly wasn't like most love stories where the guy and the girl fall in love and live happily ever after. There were no warm fuzzies and romantic sighs at all. I found it extremely sad how these two were so trapped by their addiction. So many times they would think about trying to fix it; but instead stopped out of fear. Of course neither one of them could get mad at the other, because if they did then they would need to stop and look at there own self. <br />This is Book one in the Addicted series, I can't wait to see where this journey will take Lily and Lo, and I plan to follow them every step of the way. (even knowing that it won't be an easy story to read) I did love how LIly and Lo were deeply in love with each other, and I do feel if they can get healthy and grow indivdually, then when the time is right they will have a relationship that is deeper than most people could ever imagine. Addiction though is a vicious cycle, and to get out of old patterns isn't fun or easy. I am rooting for these two, and I hope they can remain strong and come out on top when all is said and done!<br /><br /><br />This copy was given by Net Galley in exchange for an honest review..</span>
  <a data-text-id="12741308107533115957" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18369048-addicted-to-you">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Pam by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/11143936-amber-rose">Amber Rose</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=5">5</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=fucked-up-n-broken">fucked-up-n-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=darkerside-mindfuckery">darkerside-mindfuckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=not-a-typical-kinda-love">not-a-typical-kinda-love</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer766785922" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10725655964663767323"><i>5 stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Let me try to be enough for you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385339825ra/7128900.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Everyone has a story, and this is the story of Lily and Lo. Childhood friends that have grown up keeping each others secret safe and alive. <br/><br/><b>Lily<br/><blockquote><b><i>“It’s not him. It’s just the sex.”...“I’ll start shaking if I don’t find a way to satiate this. It’s like… it’s like there’s something wrong in my head, and the only way to be at ease is to do it. You understand… don’t you?”</i></b></blockquote></b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385339825i/7128901.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Lo</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>...the only girlfriend Loren Hale will ever treat well is his bottle </i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10725655964663767323" style="display:none"><i>5 stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Let me try to be enough for you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385339825ra/7128900.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everyone has a story, and this is the story of Lily and Lo. Childhood friends that have grown up keeping each others secret safe and alive. <br><br><b>Lily<br><blockquote><b><i>“It’s not him. It’s just the sex.”...“I’ll start shaking if I don’t find a way to satiate this. It’s like… it’s like there’s something wrong in my head, and the only way to be at ease is to do it. You understand… don’t you?”</i></b></blockquote></b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385339825i/7128901.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Lo</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>...the only girlfriend Loren Hale will ever treat well is his bottle of bourbon.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385339825ra/7128902.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For three years they been pretending to be in a relationship all so that their families will ever find out the real them, the one they keep hidden and sated<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>We’re in a three-year long fake relationship. We live together. He’s heard me orgasm from one room over. I’ve seen him sleep in his own puke.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>They had a system, Lil would be Lo’s designated driver, Lo would accompany Lil’s to the night clubs and bars to drown himself in alcohol while she finds her five minutes of peace in the bathroom stall. That all changes when Lily and Lo finally go after the one thing that they pray to want more than their vices, each other…BUT will it be enough???<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I need him more than he needs me. His vice is a bottle of whiskey. Mine is his body. So when we fight, I’m the one who loses out in the end.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385339825ra/7128903.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Addicted To You</b> was an amazing story about the power of addiction, the people enabling their addictions and watching the one you love hurt themselves for a few moments of peace. It goes to show that some addictions are born from circumstance and others are just in us, how could you live knowing that there is a monster you have to feed constantly, not being in control of your thoughts, actions or your body. <br><br>It was a beautifully-sad story that I absolutely loved. Lily and Lo, were so selfish in their own love for each other, resulting in another kind of addiction to add to the one they already had. I spent the first part of the book, literally pulling my hair out with the tension between the two, their addiction making them to be blind to each others attraction. I honestly can’t wait for more, not only to find out what the future holds for Lily and Lo, but to read about Lily’s other sisters and their friends. <br><br>***Review written on 11/24/2013 :) <br></span>

<div id="review_1587186999" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1587186999" />
    <a title="Chantal " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31668723-chantal"><img alt="Chantal " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464626501p2/31668723.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1587186999?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chantal " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chantal " href="/user/show/31668723-chantal">Chantal </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31668723-chantal?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31668723-chantal?shelf=mental-health">mental-health</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31668723-chantal?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31668723-chantal?shelf=listened-on-audio">listened-on-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31668723-chantal?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1587186999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3757428814681271938"><b>Maybe 2.5 stars? I am torn!</b><br/><br/>Here’s the thing about this book: Under normal circumstances I’m not sure if I would have finished it. But then, under normal circumstances I wouldn’t even have picked it up. I read this book because university is swallowing my soul whole and reading has been more of a chore recently. So I needed a book that would just absorb my attention without me having to do much thinking, a book that I wouldn’t want to put down. <b><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22296542.Addicted_to_You__Addicted___1_' title='Addicted to You (Addicted, #1) by Krista Ritchie' rel='nofollow noopener'>Addicted to You</a> is that book. It is indeed, addictin</b></span>
  <span id="freeText3757428814681271938" style="display:none"><b>Maybe 2.5 stars? I am torn!</b><br /><br />Here’s the thing about this book: Under normal circumstances I’m not sure if I would have finished it. But then, under normal circumstances I wouldn’t even have picked it up. I read this book because university is swallowing my soul whole and reading has been more of a chore recently. So I needed a book that would just absorb my attention without me having to do much thinking, a book that I wouldn’t want to put down. <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22296542.Addicted_to_You__Addicted___1_" title="Addicted to You (Addicted, #1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Addicted to You</a> is that book. It is indeed, addicting.</b><br /><br />This was definitely a “the right book at the right time” scenario and I can honestly say that I really enjoyed the reading experience, which is impressive because of how many problems I had with this book. <br /><br /><b>Let’s start with the most obvious thing about <i>Addicted to You</i>: the characters.</b> You know those characters you just want to slap in the face, take away their toys (pun intended), throw them against the wall and stomp on them screaming? That was Lily for me. <b>She was SO FRUSTRATING.</b> However, I fully appreciate that to a certain extent, this was understandable and it would have been WRONG for her not to be that way. <br /><br />Lily is <br />➢ Weak ☛ understandable<br />➢ Constantly ashamed of herself ☛ understandable<br />➢ Does not have anything even closely related to a backbone ☛ not understandable<br />➢ Let’s people walk all over her all the time ☛ not understandable<br />➢ Thinks she’s completely worthless and has the confidence of a pubescent 14-year-old ☛ kind of understandable<br /><br />Though I am by no means an expert, I know how the addiction cycle works. <b>Which is why I can forgive Lily for many things.</b> The way she pushes away her family and doesn’t want them to help? Frustrating but I get it. <b>When you’re dealing with the sort of mental disorder that requires you to keep secrets, that’s what you do. You push people away, you don’t want to admit you have a problem, you want to stay away from anyone who might come in the way of what you want to do with your life in that moment. You’ll do whatever it takes to remove pressure.</b><br /><br />And yet, <b>Lily just wasn’t a character I could root for, because there is nothing she wants in life except have sex.</b> She has no ambition, no drive, no intelligence, no strength. And that made it impossible for me to connect with her. Also<br /><br /><i>“I blushed”<br />“My elbows blushed”<br />“I turned red”<br />“My cheeks heated”<br />“I felt myself go red in the face”<br />“My entire body turned a shade of crimson”</i><br /><br />*Throws book against the wall* EVERY FREAKING PAGE. Lily stop, JUST STOP. How many times do I need to know that you blush easily and that your elbows turn red when you’re embarrassed (is that actually a thing?) and that you are constantly ashamed of yourself? I couldn’t, I just couldn’t. Ugh <br /><br /><b>Loren was a bit better, but he also wasn’t the kind of guy I was swooning over.</b> Far from it actually. However, I liked the fact that he was kind to Lily and that you could tell that he really did love her and wanted the best for her. I could muster a lot more respect for him than I could for Lily, even if he wasn’t as fleshed-out a character as I would have liked.<br /><br />Another issue I had is that <b>this book was simply too long.</b> Yes, it was entertaining. No, it wasn’t ever boring. But for goodness sake’s <b>there is only so much angst I can take in one bite before my head starts to spin.</b> This story shouldn’t have been dragged out so much, it got repetitive after a while (which I get was sort of the point but still).<br /><br />But enough complaining, because even if it seems like it from what I just wrote, I really didn’t hate this book. In fact, I suspect it’s quite a lot better than other NA books (I haven’t read many so I can’t be sure). So here are the (many) things this book did RIGHT:<br /><br />✔︎ It is <b>devoid of slut-shaming (beyond what Lily thinks of herself) and girl-hate</b> <br />✔︎ Lo’s and Lily’s relationship is incredibly toxic and the book acknowledges that. <b>Addiction is never romanticised.</b><br />✔︎ <b>Family plays a big role</b> in this book and I loved seeing the dynamics between the different sisters.<br />✔︎ The book is a very <b>realistic portrayal of addiction</b>.<br />✔︎ <b>I loved Rose and Connor.</b> Great job on the side characters<br />✔︎ The last 15% were really strong. <b>Well-handled and a positive message.</b><br /><br /><b>Even if I found this book a bit infuriating at times, I definitely recommend it if you’re looking for a new NA book to read or just need something to get you out of the reading slump. It will definitely do the trick.</b><br /><br />As for me, I don’t plan on continuing on with this series, however, I am very interested in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20658510.Kiss_the_Sky__Calloway_Sisters___1__Addicted___2_1_" title="Kiss the Sky (Calloway Sisters, #1; Addicted, #2.1) by Krista Ritchie" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss the Sky</a> because I think that one will be way more up my alley. So my question is, is it possible to read that one without continuing with the Addicted series? Let me know! </span>
  <a data-text-id="3757428814681271938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/6U1gsIZZZ6OZqI7i9aTAotZLGtm1u5V0E4dZdArcGY40PeaF53g90DY5FdGh3YQDu2RTy2PkP5ghPpUeCAPaA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kxjRzyrlDHKRuR10140+TyTndZBvCsRn4Oz3tGKro7xUbRPX/2GJG18HWxga3NtdoVPItCRTusxQJhCFyqDcsg==')})
  }
//]]>
